          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=were">were</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=sos-bookshelf-bingo">sos-bookshelf-bingo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=fae">fae</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=zzread-mar-2011">zzread-mar-2011</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer119701989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3548958438515076938">The Mercy Thompson series is a comfort read for me. I sit down and immerse myself in the Mercy’s world and I don’t even notice that time has passed. In fact, I am always sad when I finish reading a book. Not because the ending is sad, but because I finished another book in the series. I don't want this series to end.<br/><br/>I love so many things about this series. I love how the author mixes up werewolves, vampires, and fae and has them living together in our world semi-peacefully. I enjoy the pack hier</span>
  <span id="freeText3548958438515076938" style="display:none">The Mercy Thompson series is a comfort read for me. I sit down and immerse myself in the Mercy’s world and I don’t even notice that time has passed. In fact, I am always sad when I finish reading a book. Not because the ending is sad, but because I finished another book in the series. I don't want this series to end.<br /><br />I love so many things about this series. I love how the author mixes up werewolves, vampires, and fae and has them living together in our world semi-peacefully. I enjoy the pack hierarchy, the politics between the vampires and the wolves, and the fae magic. <br /><br />Bone Crossed begins a week after Iron Kissed. Mercy is damaged, and subject to panic attacks. Everyone walks on eggshells around her. Marsilia the Vampire Queen is out to kill Mercy. Mercy’s mom even comes to visit. Mercy’s Scooby Doo loving vampire pal Stefan has been “dehydrated” and dropped at her doorstep. Mercy’s friend Amber in Spokane has a problem with ghosts. Mercy decides to go to Spokane for her safety. <br /><br />My favorite scenes involved Amber’s son Chad. I loved the interactions between Mercy and Chad, especially when they were playing a rather competitive game of Battleship. <br /><br />The Mercy Thompson series has great characters. Stefan is one of my favorites and his character is further developed in this installment. Stefan is a faithful friend to Mercy and uses his vampire powers to protect her. Marsilia the Vampire Queen is conniving, devious, and deadly. I enjoyed the addition of the Oak Man. The Oak Man helped explain the purpose of the walking stick that follows Mercy around. <br /><br />This book had many touching moments. Adam and Mercy’s relationship progresses slowly and she becomes his mate:<br /><blockquote> “From this day forward…Mine to me and mine. Pack and only lover.”</blockquote><br />There was another point where Mercy has a revelation about her relationship to Adam. She realizes that he does love her and at that point she asserts her position in the pack. I loved that moment - "Mine."<br /><br />I’m looking forward to reading the next book in the series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3548958438515076938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3272631106247419580">Yay, Stefan's back in this book! Since he is my favorite character in the series, I seriously missed him in the last book. And, he is better than ever. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Want to explain to the kid that I'm more a Spike than a Buffy? A villain, not a superhero?"<br/>I batted my eyelashes at him. "You're my hero."...<br/>"I'm no one's hero, Mercy."<br/>I turned my face until I was looking directly at Chad. "Do you think that means I won't get to see him in spandex?"...   <span id="freeText3272631106247419580" style="display:none">Yay, Stefan's back in this book! Since he is my favorite character in the series, I seriously missed him in the last book. And, he is better than ever. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Want to explain to the kid that I'm more a Spike than a Buffy? A villain, not a superhero?"<br>I batted my eyelashes at him. "You're my hero."...<br>"I'm no one's hero, Mercy."<br>I turned my face until I was looking directly at Chad. "Do you think that means I won't get to see him in spandex?"... Chad made a yuck face.<br>"hey," I told them, "watching good-looking men run around in tight-fitting costumes is high on my list of things I'd like to do before I die."</i>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426030616i/13965092._SX540_.jpg" alt="thor and loki photo: Loki and Thor Avengers thor-vs-loki.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>yeah, me too...<br><br>So, in this book, we have Mercy dealing with the aftermath of her attack in the last book. She has panic attacks and flashbacks, but still, I would say that it would have been much better to just not have the whole rape thing in the storyline because I feel like it is way too light to be respectful of real rape victims. As a matter of fact, let me just state that I would be happy if there were no rape scenes at all. In real life or books.<br><br>The story in this book goes back to the vampires with Marsilia going after Mercy and marking her for death with a skull and crossbones type of thing on her door. This propels Mercy in to leaving town, right in to the clutches of a whole new set of problems - and things that want to kill her. This girl has a hella lot of creatures that want to kill her!<br><br>I liked the overall plotline, but mostly liked Stefan in the book, along with the little boy. I am hopeful that the next book or so will give us something that makes Samuel happy because he deserves it.<br></span>

<div id="review_1896541643" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1896541643" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1896541643?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1896541643" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16206919213080451712"><b>1st Read July 2010</b><br/><b>2nd Read March 2014</b> <br/><b>3rd Read January 2016</b><br/><b>4th Read January 2017</b> <br/><b>5th Read February 2018</b><br/><br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/>When Stephan appears in Mercy's trailer on the verge of death she discovers that Marsilia (queen of the local vampire seethe) has found out about the vampire that Mercy killed. To say that Marsilia is unhappy is an understatement. Stephan has been thrown out of the seethe for helping keep Mercy's secret & Marsilia wants blood - preferably Mercy's but she is happy to target her fr</span>
  <span id="freeText16206919213080451712" style="display:none"><b>1st Read July 2010</b><br /><b>2nd Read March 2014</b> <br /><b>3rd Read January 2016</b><br /><b>4th Read January 2017</b> <br /><b>5th Read February 2018</b><br /><br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br />When Stephan appears in Mercy's trailer on the verge of death she discovers that Marsilia (queen of the local vampire seethe) has found out about the vampire that Mercy killed. To say that Marsilia is unhappy is an understatement. Stephan has been thrown out of the seethe for helping keep Mercy's secret &amp; Marsilia wants blood - preferably Mercy's but she is happy to target her friends too. With Adam &amp; Samuel determined to keep her safe it looks like this could be the start of a war between the werewolves and the vampires. When Mercy's friend from college Amber turns up asking for Mercy's help dealing with a ghost everyone thinks this would be the perfect way to get Mercy out of Marsilia's reach. But nothing is as it seems and Mercy soon finds she has jumped out of the frying pan straight into the fire.<br /><br />I'm a big fan of <b>Patricia Briggs</b> and love the Mercy Thompson series so was really looking forward to reading <b>Bone Crossed</b> &amp; I wasn't disappointed. I love Mercy and was devastated for her at the end of the last book so I really wanted to know how she was getting on. A week after the ending of <b>Iron Kissed</b> Mercy is in a mess both emotionally and physically, suffering regularly from panic attacks and flashbacks of the event. She knows she loves Adam but she is finding it hard to allow him to get close to her and I felt her reactions were very realistic considering what she has been through. I've always had a soft spot for Adam but he is so patient and caring towards Mercy in this book that I couldn't help liking him even more. He understands what she is going through and is determined to help her recover.<br /><br />Spending time in Mercy's world is like visiting with friends and I always find myself easily slipping into her world like I never left. I love each of the characters in their own ways and even the more minor characters like Jesse and Warren are so well rounded that it feels like you actually know them. If I had one minor disappointment it was that I would have liked to have spent a little more time with Stephan in this installment of the series, especially as the main plot revolves around the vampires. He suffers so much in <b>Bone Crossed</b> and I hope we get to see how he deals with the things Marsilia has done over the next few books. We didn't see that much of Samuel either but that was more understandable considering the plot but we get to see a lot of Adam so that makes up for it!<br /><br />If you're yet to discover the Mercy Thompson series then I would highly recommend it to urban fantasy fans. It is one of my favorite series and Mercy is a fantastic heroine. Although you could probably read this as a stand alone novel I would strongly recommend reading the series in order so you don't miss any of the back story. If you're already a fan of the series &amp; haven't already read <b>Bone Crossed</b> what are you waiting for? This was probably my favorite book in the series so far so I'm sure you're going to enjoy it!<br /><br />___________________________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />Buddy reread with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/874487653" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a><br /><br />No time to write another review - must carry on reading the series :o) You'll have to read the old one if you want to know more!<br /><br />___________________________________<br /><br /><b>3rd Read</b><br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561631923" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a><br /><br />Since it's been nearly 2 years since Ange &amp; I buddy read this series last we decided we're well overdue another read in the run up to the release of Fire Touched next March.<br /><br />I love this series so much! The characters, the world building just everything about these books makes them a comfort read for me. Along with Ilona Andrews's Kate Daniels series this is probably my most reread series &amp; I never get tired of it.<br /><br />___________________________________<br /><br /><b>4th Read</b><br /><br />Mercy has such a knack for getting herself in trouble that it's impressive really. I think Adam sums it up perfectly in one sentence <i>“Only you could go to Spokane and get bitten by the one vampire in the whole city.”</i> Bloody vampires can never be trusted, especially not around our favourite trouble magnet but it makes for fun reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16206919213080451712" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/37639584?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie Collins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie Collins" href="/user/show/321673-jamie-collins">Jamie Collins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780441016761" href="/book/show/3413662-bone-crossed">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/321673-jamie-collins?shelf=fantasy-urban">fantasy-urban</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer37639584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1173447652697449545">This was a pretty good read, but not as satisfying as the earlier books. Why is there always a drop in quality when these series move into hardback?<br/><br/>First of all, this book picks up right where the previous one left off, as if the action had been uninterrupted. It didn't feel like an opening chapter, but rather like I had opened a book in the middle and picked a chapter at random. The emotional intensity of the earlier books is missing here, particularly in Mercy's interaction with Stefan. The bo</span>
  <span id="freeText1173447652697449545" style="display:none">This was a pretty good read, but not as satisfying as the earlier books. Why is there always a drop in quality when these series move into hardback?<br /><br />First of all, this book picks up right where the previous one left off, as if the action had been uninterrupted. It didn't feel like an opening chapter, but rather like I had opened a book in the middle and picked a chapter at random. The emotional intensity of the earlier books is missing here, particularly in Mercy's interaction with Stefan. The book is too short and too crowded with characters for the author to spend enough time on any one of them. It reminded me a little of a Laurell Hamilton book, which is not a good thing.<br /><br />The first third of the novel has an almost frantic level of activity, but the pace thankfully slows after that and the story begins to have more of the feel of the previous Mercy books. I did like the overall plot, and I like Stefan. I wish the author had spent more time fleshing out his character. The book could have used another 100 pages.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1173447652697449545" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12475267702863115119"><b>5 "phenomenal" stars.</b>🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><br/>What do you say about a series that just keeps getting better and better ....I am absolutely addicted at this point!!!!...to this fabulous and stellar paranormal/fantasy series....... I finish one book and I immediately want to pick up the next!!!!<br/><br/>I just have to know what is going to be next for Mercy Thompson our kick-ass heroine/car mechanic/ skinwalker & coyote-shifter.<br/><br/>I was delighted to see the return of Stefan (Mercy's Vampire friend) for this story and I loved how</span>
  <span id="freeText12475267702863115119" style="display:none"><b>5 "phenomenal" stars.</b>🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br /><br />What do you say about a series that just keeps getting better and better ....I am absolutely addicted at this point!!!!...to this fabulous and stellar paranormal/fantasy series....... I finish one book and I immediately want to pick up the next!!!!<br /><br />I just have to know what is going to be next for Mercy Thompson our kick-ass heroine/car mechanic/ skinwalker &amp; coyote-shifter.<br /><br />I was delighted to see the return of Stefan (Mercy's Vampire friend) for this story and I loved how he came through for our heroine when she really needed him .......in an intense face-off with Marsilia (Queen of the local Vampire seethe).<br />I have such a soft spot for Stefan...I find his loyalty to his friends incredibly endearing and kind of on a par with Mercy's own intensity ....she is always there for her friends and also the deserving....even if it costs her dearly.<br /><br />I am loving Adam plenty too...but surely.... that simply goes without saying!!!! ....a considerate Alpha....do they really make those???<br /><br />A FANTASTIC READ.<br /><br /><b>Favorite Highlights:</b> <br /> <i>....But you can’t marry someone to fix him, even if you love them. And I didn’t love Samuel the way a woman should love her mate, the way I loved Adam. Samuel didn’t love me that way either. Close, but not quite. And except in horseshoes and hand grenades, close doesn’t count.<br /><br />.....People I cared about could hurt my feelings, but almost complete strangers? I could care less about what they thought.<br /><br />.....He was teasing ... but serious as well. One of the oddest things about being grown-up was looking back at something you thought you knew and finding out the truth of it was completely different from what you had always believed. </i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1931847733804767243">I know I said this about <i>Iron Kissed</i>, but I think this might be my favourite in the series! Mercy is now a firmly one of my favourite heroines, the plot was interesting and kept me guessing and Adam was wicked hot. For me this series gets better and better as you learn more and more about paranormal world the Mercy seems to keep getting mixed up in.<br /><br />I <i>do</i> seem to be developing another crush as well, does anyone else have the hots for Bran?</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6638639996360543415"><b>3.5</b><br/><br/>Figures, the moment I think about giving up with this series, the 4th picks up!!!<br/><br/>Liked it much more than all the others, simply because Adam and Mercy interact with each other. I don't need sex in the books, that's why I love reading YA books, but I do need for both main characters have some sort of communication. And this book gave me that. And still, I like more the vamps in this series than werewolves. And I usually go for furry animals and not blood sucking ones. <br/><br/>Definitely will continue </span>
  <span id="freeText6638639996360543415" style="display:none"><b>3.5</b><br /><br />Figures, the moment I think about giving up with this series, the 4th picks up!!!<br /><br />Liked it much more than all the others, simply because Adam and Mercy interact with each other. I don't need sex in the books, that's why I love reading YA books, but I do need for both main characters have some sort of communication. And this book gave me that. And still, I like more the vamps in this series than werewolves. And I usually go for furry animals and not blood sucking ones. <br /><br />Definitely will continue with the series, but I am gonna pause for some time... </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aU9oFgot7+Lg7xMURpT0Mm8Z/de7RZHvyTcozMNKpzXJkBeN5H5j70QX7+XgleYDcEJA2laVYjc0NS40eHwHeQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('32E5PGq5+eftmk2Hxj8rH56x3K8QKiLBLdtVmVVZZJh/vkanhOp16klisXZgPjkugephov360RnQ2VNh7m/E1A==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer9307958451375280661"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br/><br/>Patricia Briggs was born in Butte, Montana, to a children’s librarian who passed on to her kids a love of reading and books. Patricia grew up reading fairy tales and books about horses, and later developed an interest in folklore and history. When she decided to write a book of her own, a fantasy book seemed a n</span>
  <span id="freeText9307958451375280661" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br /><br />Patricia Briggs was born in Butte, Montana, to a children’s librarian who passed on to her kids a love of reading and books. Patricia grew up reading fairy tales and books about horses, and later developed an interest in folklore and history. When she decided to write a book of her own, a fantasy book seemed a natural choice. Patricia graduated from Montana State University with degrees in history and German and she worked for a while as a substitute teacher. Currently, she lives in Montana with her husband, children, and six horses and writes full time, much to the delight of her fans.</span>
